The NewTLSConfig factory function converts this configuration into a standard Go tls.Config with proper certificate loading, CA chain validation, and client certificate handling.\\n\\n## Configuration Embedding\\nTLSConfig is embedded within the HTTPClientConfig struct and wired into all major Prometheus configuration types:\\n- ScrapeConfig: Enables TLS for scraping targets\\n- RemoteWriteConfig: Enables TLS for remote write endpoints\\n- RemoteReadConfig: Enables TLS for remote read endpoints\\n- AlertmanagerConfig: Enables TLS for alertmanager communication\\n- TracingConfig: Contains TLSConfig for OTLP tracing exporters\\n\\n## Client-Side TLS Application\\nThe prometheus/prometheus codebase applies TLS configuration at multiple layers:\\n- scrape/scrape.go: Uses config_util.NewClientFromConfig to create HTTP clients with TLS for target scraping\\n- storage/remote/client.go, write.go, storage.go: Apply HTTPClientConfig with TLS for remote storage operations\\n- tracing/tracing.go: Applies TLSConfig to both gRPC (via credentials.NewTLS) and HTTP OTLP exporters\\n\\n## Server-Side TLS Setup\\nThe web server TLS is configured via:\\n- web/web.go: Invokes toolkit_web.ServeMultiple, which uses the exporter-toolkit library to handle server-side TLS based on a web configuration file\\n- cmd/prometheus/main.go: Passes the webConfig parameter to enable server TLS\\n\\n## Service Discovery Plugin TLS Support\\nService discovery plugins implement TLS support through embedded HTTPClientConfig:\\n- discovery/kubernetes/kubernetes.go: Kubernetes SD uses HTTPClientConfig for API server communication\\n- discovery/consul/consul.go: Consul SD uses HTTPClientConfig for HTTP API calls\\n- Additional SDs (AWS, Azure, DNS, HTTP, etc.) follow the same pattern\\n\\n## TLS Validation and Verification\\nThe promtool CLI validates TLS configuration across the stack:\\n- cmd/promtool/main.go CheckWebConfig: Validates web server TLS configuration files\\n- cmd/promtool/main.go checkTLSConfig: Validates TLS settings for scrape targets, remote endpoints, alertmanagers, and service discovery plugins\\n- Validation ensures cert/key file pairs are properly specified and files exist\\n- Config loading applies validation to all HTTPClientConfig instances through the Validate() method\\n\\nThis unified approach ensures TLS is consistently enforced on all external interfaces, from target scraping to remote storage communication, tracing exporters, service discovery, and the web server itself.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Architecture Across the Prometheus Stack\\n\\nThe Prometheus monitoring stack enforces TLS configuration across all external-facing interfaces through a unified architecture centered on the TLSConfig struct defined in the prometheus-common library.\\n\\n## TLS Struct Definition (Canonical)\\nThe canonical TLSConfig struct is defined in `sourcegraph-testing/prometheus-common/config/http_config.go` and includes: CAFile, CertFile, KeyFile, ServerName, and InsecureSkipVerify. The NewTLSConfig factory function converts this configuration into a standard Go tls.Config with proper certificate loading, CA chain validation, and client certificate handling.\\n\\n## Configuration Embedding\\nTLSConfig is embedded within the HTTPClientConfig struct and wired into all major Prometheus configuration types:\\n- ScrapeConfig: Enables TLS for scraping targets\\n- RemoteWriteConfig: Enables TLS for remote write endpoints\\n- RemoteReadConfig: Enables TLS for remote read endpoints\\n- AlertmanagerConfig: Enables TLS for alertmanager communication\\n- TracingConfig: Contains TLSConfig for OTLP tracing exporters\\n\\n## Client-Side TLS Application\\nThe prometheus/prometheus codebase applies TLS configuration at multiple layers:\\n- scrape/scrape.go: Uses config_util.NewClientFromConfig to create HTTP clients with TLS for target scraping\\n- storage/remote/client.go, write.go, storage.go: Apply HTTPClientConfig with TLS for remote storage operations\\n- tracing/tracing.go: Applies TLSConfig to both gRPC (via credentials.NewTLS) and HTTP OTLP exporters\\n\\n## Server-Side TLS Setup\\nThe web server TLS is configured via:\\n- web/web.go: Invokes toolkit_web.ServeMultiple, which uses the exporter-toolkit library to handle server-side TLS based on a web configuration file\\n- cmd/prometheus/main.go: Passes the webConfig parameter to enable server TLS\\n\\n## Service Discovery Plugin TLS Support\\nService discovery plugins implement TLS support through embedded HTTPClientConfig:\\n- discovery/kubernetes/kubernetes.go: Kubernetes SD uses HTTPClientConfig for API server communication\\n- discovery/consul/consul.go: Consul SD uses HTTPClientConfig for HTTP API calls\\n- Additional SDs (AWS, Azure, DNS, HTTP, etc.) follow the
